BUG: This should be conditional on the component type\n    if val.endswith('%'):\n        val = val[:-1]\n        mult = 255.0 / 100\n\n    try:\n        return int(float(val) * mult)\n    except ValueError:\n        raise ValueError(\"must be a valid color value\")\n\n\n# Recreate the CORRECT _parse_value method as it should be\ndef correct_parse_value(kind: str, val: str) -> int:\n    \"\"\"\n    This is the CORRECT version with the fix applied.\n\n    Fix: The method now takes a 'kind' parameter that specifies which\n    component is being parsed ('h' for hue, 's' for saturation, 'v' for value).\n    For hue, use 359.0 as the max. For saturation/value, use 255.0.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        return int(val)\n    except ValueError:\n        pass\n\n    mult = 359.0 if kind == 'h' else 255.0  # FIX: Use 359 for hue, 255 for others\n    if val.endswith('%'):\n        val = val[:-1]\n        mult = mult / 100\n\n    try:\n        return int(float(val) * mult)\n    except ValueError:\n        raise ValueError(\"must be a valid color value\")\n\n\ndef buggy_parse_hsv(color_string: str) -> tuple:\n    \"\"\"\n    Parse HSV/HSVA color string using the buggy method.\n\n    This demonstrates the bug where all components are scaled by 255.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not color_string.startswith(('hsv(', 'hsva(')) or not color_string.endswith(')'):\n        raise ValueError(f\"Invalid color string: {color_string}\")\n\n    # Hue: 100% of 359 = 359\n        # - Saturation: 100% of 255 = 255\n        # - Value: 100% of 255 = 255\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        result = color_parser.to_py('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n        expected = QColor.fromHsv(359, 255, 255)\n\n        assert result.getHsv() == expected.getHsv(), (\n            f\"Expected hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) to parse as {expected.getHsv()}, \"\n            f\"but got {result.getHsv()}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_hsv_50_percent_hue(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) correctly scales hue to 179.\"\"\"\n        # When all values are 50%, we expect:\n        # - Hue: 50% of 359 = 179.5 ≈ 179 or 180\n        # - Saturation: 50% of 255 = 127.5 ≈ 127 or 128\n        # - Value: 50% of 255 = 127.5 ≈ 127 or 128\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        result = color_parser.to_py('hsv(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n        h, s, v, _ = result.getHsv()\n\n        # Hue should be around 179-180 (50% of 359)\n        assert 179 <= h <= 180, (\n            f\"Expected hue to be around 179-180 (50% of 359), but got {h}\"\n        )\n        # Saturation should be around 127-128 (50% of 255)\n        assert 127 <= s <= 128, (\n            f\"Expected saturation to be around 127-128 (50% of 255), but got {s}\"\n        )\n        # Value should be around 127-128 (50% of 255)\n        assert 127 <= v <= 128, (\n            f\"Expected value to be around 127-128 (50% of 255), but got {v}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_hsv_10_percent(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsv(10%, 10%, 10%) correctly scales all components.\"\"\"\n        # When all values are 10%, we expect:\n        # - Hue: 10% of 359 = 35.9 ≈ 35\n        # - Saturation: 10% of 255 = 25.5 ≈ 25 or 26\n        # - Value: 10% of 255 = 25.5 ≈ 25 or 26\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        result = color_parser.to_py('hsv(10%, 10%, 10%)')\n        h, s, v, _ = result.getHsv()\n\n        # Hue should be around 35-36 (10% of 359)\n        assert 35 <= h <= 36, (\n            f\"Expected hue to be around 35-36 (10% of 359), but got {h}\"\n        )\n        # Saturation should be around 25-26 (10% of 255)\n        assert 25 <= s <= 26, (\n            f\"Expected saturation to be around 25-26 (10% of 255), but got {s}\"\n        )\n        # Value should be around 25-26 (10% of 255)\n        assert 25 <= v <= 26, (\n            f\"Expected value to be around 25-26 (10% of 255), but got {v}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_hsva_100_percent_all_channels(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsva(100%, 100%, 100%, 100%) correctly scales all channels.\"\"\"\n        # When all values are 100%, we expect:\n        # - Hue: 100% of 359 = 359\n        # - Saturation: 100% of 255 = 255\n        # - Value: 100% of 255 = 255\n        # - Alpha: 100% of 255 = 255\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        result = color_parser.to_py('hsva(100%, 100%, 100%, 100%)')\n        expected = QColor.fromHsv(359, 255, 255, 255)\n\n        assert result.getHsv() == expected.getHsv(), (\n            f\"Expected hsva(100%, 100%, 100%, 100%) to parse as {expected.getHsv()}, \"\n            f\"but got {result.getHsv()}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_hsva_50_percent_all_channels(self):\n        \"\"\"Test that hsva(50%, 50%, 50%, 50%) correctly scales all channels.\"\"\"\n        # When all values are 50%, we expect:\n        # - Hue: 50% of 359 = 179.5 ≈ 179 or 180\n        # - Saturation: 50% of 255 = 127.5 ≈ 127 or 128\n        # - Value: 50% of 255 = 127.5 ≈ 127 or 128\n        # - Alpha: 50% of 255 = 127.5 ≈ 127 or 128\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        result = color_parser.to_py('hsva(50%, 50%, 50%, 50%)')\n        h, s, v, a = result.getHsv()\n\n        # Hue should be around 179-180 (50% of 359)\n        assert 179 <= h <= 180, (\n            f\"Expected hue to be around 179-180 (50% of 359), but got {h}\"\n        )\n        # Saturation should be around 127-128 (50% of 255)\n        assert 127 <= s <= 128, (\n            f\"Expected saturation to be around 127-128 (50% of 255), but got {s}\"\n        )\n        # Value should be around 127-128 (50% of 255)\n        assert 127 <= v <= 128, (\n            f\"Expected value to be around 127-128 (50% of 255), but got {v}\"\n        )\n        # Alpha should be around 127-128 (50% of 255)\n        assert 127 <= a <= 128, (\n            f\"Expected alpha to be around 127-128 (50% of 255), but got {a}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_hsva_with_mixed_percentages(self):\n        \"\"\"Test hsva with different percentages for each channel.\"\"\"\n        # hsva(20%, 30%, 40%, 50%):\n        # - Hue: 20% of 359 = 71.8 ≈ 71 or 72\n        # - Saturation: 30% of 255 = 76.5 ≈ 76 or 77\n        # - Value: 40% of 255 = 102 ≈ 102\n        # - Alpha: 50% of 255 = 127.5 ≈ 127 or 128\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        result = color_parser.to_py('hsva(20%, 30%, 40%, 50%)')\n        h, s, v, a = result.getHsv()\n\n        # Hue should be around 71-72 (20% of 359)\n        assert 71 <= h <= 72, (\n            f\"Expected hue to be around 71-72 (20% of 359), but got {h}\"\n        )\n        # Saturation should be around 76-77 (30% of 255)\n        assert 76 <= s <= 77, (\n            f\"Expected saturation to be around 76-77 (30% of 255), but got {s}\"\n        )\n        # Value should be around 102 (40% of 255)\n        assert 102 <= v <= 103, (\n            f\"Expected value to be around 102-103 (40% of 255), but got {v}\"\n        )\n        # Alpha should be around 127-128 (50% of 255)\n        assert 127 <= a <= 128, (\n            f\"Expected alpha to be around 127-128 (50% of 255), but got {a}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_hue_scaling_differs_from_saturation_value(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Verify that hue scaling is different from saturation/value scaling.\n\n        This test directly checks that the hue component uses 0-359 range,\n        while saturation and value use 0-255 range. If hue is incorrectly\n        using 255 as the max, this test will fail.\n        \"\"\"\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        # For 100% input:\n        # - If hue uses 255: result would be ~255\n        # - If hue uses 359: result would be 359\n        result = color_parser.to_py('hsv(100%, 0%, 0%)')\n        h, _, _, _ = result.getHsv()\n\n        # Hue at 100% should be 359 (the full hue range)\n        assert h == 359, (\n            f\"HSV hue at 100% should be 359, not 255. Got {h}. \"\n            f\"This indicates the bug where hue is scaled by 255 instead of 359.\"\n        )\n\n    def test_hsv_25_percent_hue_distinct(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Test that 25% hue is different when using 359 vs 255 scaling.\n\n        - With correct 359 scaling: 25% of 359 = 89.75 ≈ 89 or 90\n        - With buggy 255 scaling: 25% of 255 = 63.75 ≈ 63 or 64\n\n        The difference is clear: 89-90 vs 63-64\n        \"\"\"\n        color_parser = configtypes.QtColor()\n        result = color_parser.to_py('hsv(25%, 0%, 0%)')\n        h, _, _, _ = result.getHsv()\n\n        # Correct hue should be around 89-90\n        assert 89 <= h <= 90, (\n            f\"Expected hue for 25% to be around 89-90 (25% of 359), but got {h}. \"\n            f\"If you got 63-64, the bug is present (25% of 255 instead of 359).\"\n        )\n\n\nif __name__ == '__main__':\n    # Run tests with pytest\n    pytest.main([__file__, '-v'])\n"}}

BUG: This should be conditional on the component type\n    if val.endswith('%'):\n        val = val[:-1]\n        mult = 255.0 / 100\n\n    try:\n        return int(float(val) * mult)\n    except ValueError:\n        raise ValueError(\"must be a valid color value\")\n\n\n# Recreate the CORRECT _parse_value method as it should be\ndef correct_parse_value(kind: str, val: str) -> int:\n    \"\"\"\n    This is the CORRECT version with the fix applied.\n\n    Fix: The method now takes a 'kind' parameter that specifies which\n    component is being parsed ('h' for hue, 's' for saturation, 'v' for value).\n    For hue, use 359.0 as the max. For saturation/value, use 255.0.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        return int(val)\n    except ValueError:\n        pass\n\n    mult = 359.0 if kind == 'h' else 255.0  # FIX: Use 359 for hue, 255 for others\n    if val.endswith('%'):\n        val = val[:-1]\n        mult = mult / 100\n\n    try:\n        return int(float(val) * mult)\n    except ValueError:\n        raise ValueError(\"must be a valid color value\")\n\n\ndef buggy_parse_hsv(color_string: str) -> tuple:\n    \"\"\"\n    Parse HSV/HSVA color string using the buggy method.\n\n    This demonstrates the bug where all components are scaled by 255.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not color_string.startswith(('hsv(', 'hsva(')) or not color_string.endswith(')'):\n        raise ValueError(f\"Invalid color string: {color_string}\")\n\n    # Extract the color type and values\n    if '(' in color_string:\n        openparen = color_string.index('(')\n        kind = color_string[:openparen]\n        vals_str = color_string[openparen+1:-1]\n        vals = [v.strip() for v in vals_str.split(',')]\n\n        # Parse values using the correct method, passing the component type\n        int_vals = [correct_parse_value(p[0], p[1]) for p in zip(kind, vals)]\n        return tuple(int_vals)\n\n    raise ValueError(f\"Could not parse: {color_string}\")\n\n\nclass TestHSVPercentageBug:\n    \"\"\"\n    Test that demonstrates the HSV percentage parsing bug.\n\n    The bug is that hue (which should have a range of 0-359 degrees)\n    is incorrectly scaled using 255 as the maximum instead of 359.\n\n    The buggy version produces:\n    - hsv(100%, 100%, 100%) -> (255, 255, 255) instead of (359, 255, 255)\n    - hsv(50%, 50%, 50%) -> (127, 127, 127) instead of (179, 127, 127)\n\n    The correct version should produce the right values.\n    \"\"\"\n\n    def test_bug_hsv_100_percent_hue_vs_saturation(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Demonstrate the bug: 100% hue produces 255 instead of 359.\n\n        This is the CORE bug:\n        - Hue should use 0-359 range (degrees)\n        - Saturation/Value should use 0-255 range\n\n        With the bug, 100% of both hue and saturation produce the same value (255),\n        which is incorrect.\n        \"\"\"\n        buggy_result = buggy_parse_hsv('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n        correct_result = correct_parse_hsv('hsv(100%, 100%, 100%)')\n\n        # Buggy: {buggy_v}, Correct: {correct_v}\"\n        )\n\n    def test_rgb_parsing_not_affected(self):\n        \"\"\"\n        Verify that RGB parsing (which all components should be 0-255) works the same\n        in both buggy and correct versions.\n        \"\"\"\n        # RGB doesn't have the hue scaling issue since all components use 0-255\n        def buggy_parse_rgb(color_string: str) -> tuple:\n            if not color_string.startswith('rgb(') or not color_string.endswith(')'):\n                raise ValueError(f\"Invalid color string: {color_string}\")\n            vals_str = color_string[4:-1]\n            vals = [v.strip() for v in vals_str.split(',')]\n            return tuple(buggy_parse_value(v) for v in vals)\n\n        def correct_parse_rgb(color_string: str) -> tuple:\n            if not color_string.startswith('rgb(') or not color_string.endswith(')'):\n                raise ValueError(f\"Invalid color string: {color_string}\")\n            vals_str = color_string[4:-1]\n            vals = [v.strip() for v in vals_str.split(',')]\n            # For RGB, all components are 'r', 'g', 'b' which are not 'h'\n            # So they all use 255.0 as the multiplier\n            return tuple(correct_parse_value('r' if i == 0 else ('g' if i == 1 else 'b'), v)\n                        for i, v in enumerate(vals))\n\n        buggy_rgb = buggy_parse_rgb('rgb(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n        correct_rgb = correct_parse_rgb('rgb(50%, 50%, 50%)')\n\n        # All components should be around 127-128\n        for val in buggy_rgb:\n            assert 127 <= val <= 128, f\"Buggy RGB should be around 127-128, got {buggy_rgb}\"\n        for val in correct_rgb:\n            assert 127 <= val <= 128, f\"Correct RGB should be around 127-128, got {correct_rgb}\"\n\n        # They should be identical for RGB\n        assert buggy_rgb == correct_rgb, (\n            f\"RGB parsing should be identical. BUG: This should be conditional on the component type\n    if val.endswith('%'):\n        val = val[:-1]\n        mult = 255.0 / 100\n\n    try:\n        return int(float(val) * mult)\n    except ValueError:\n        raise ValueError(\"must be a valid color value\")\n\n\n# Recreate the CORRECT _parse_value method as it should be\ndef correct_parse_value(kind: str, val: str) -> int:\n    \"\"\"\n    This is the CORRECT version with the fix applied.\n\n    Fix: The method now takes a 'kind' parameter that specifies which\n    component is being parsed ('h' for hue, 's' for saturation, 'v' for value).\n    For hue, use 359.0 as the max. For saturation/value, use 255.0.\n    \"\"\"\n    try:\n        return int(val)\n    except ValueError:\n        pass\n\n    mult = 359.0 if kind == 'h' else 255.0  # FIX: Use 359 for hue, 255 for others\n    if val.endswith('%'):\n        val = val[:-1]\n        mult = mult / 100\n\n    try:\n        return int(float(val) * mult)\n    except ValueError:\n        raise ValueError(\"must be a valid color value\")\n\n\ndef buggy_parse_hsv(color_string: str) -> tuple:\n    \"\"\"\n    Parse HSV/HSVA color string using the buggy method.\n\n    This demonstrates the bug where all components are scaled by 255.\n    \"\"\"\n    if not color_string.startswith(('hsv(', 'hsva(')) or not color_string.endswith(')'):\n        raise ValueError(f\"Invalid color string: {color_string}\")\n\n    # Extract the color type and values\n    if '(' in color_string:\n        openparen = color_string.index('(')\n        kind = color_string[:openparen]\n        vals_str = color_string[openparen+1:-1]\n        vals = [v.strip() for v in vals_str.split(',')]\n\n        #
